Navigation

Functional

get

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Basic examples](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#basic-examples)
    
*   [Usage](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#usage)
    
*   [Resources](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#resources)
    
*   [Block parameters](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#block-parameters)
    
*   [Using {{else}}](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#using-else)
    
*   [Attributes](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#attributes)
    
*   [limit](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#limit)
    
*   [page](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#page)
    
*   [order](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#order)
    
*   [include](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#include)
    
*   [filter](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#filter)
    
*   [Passing data to filter](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#passing-data-to-filter)
    
*   [Filtering by primary tag](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#filtering-by-primary-tag)
    
*   [Filtering by primary author](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#filtering-by-primary-author)
    
*   [Filtering by membership type](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#filtering-by-membership-type)
    
*   [Filtering by tier visibility](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#filtering-by-tier-visibility)
    

* * *

`{{#get}}` is a special block helper that makes a custom query to the Ghost API to fetch publicly available data. These requests are made server-side before your templates are rendered. This means you can fetch additional data, separate from what is provided by [default in each context](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/contexts)
. In its most basic form, the `{{#get}}` helper performs a “browse” query that creates a block of data that represents a list of your **posts**, **authors**, **tags**, or **tiers**. Use the `{{#foreach}}` helper to iterate over this block of data. The `{{#get}}` helper can also be used to perform a “read” query that fetches one specific author, post, tag, or tier when the relevant _resource field_ - e.g., **id** or **slug** – is provided as an attribute.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#basic-examples)

Basic examples

Get the 15 newest posts from the API.

    {{#get "posts"}}
        {{#foreach posts}}
            {{title}}
        {{/foreach}}
    {{/get}}
    

Get a single post with the id of 2, including its related tags and author data, using a block parameter. Learn more about [block parameters](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#block-parameters)
 below.

    {{#get "posts" id="2" include="tags,authors" as |post|}}
        {{#post}}
            {{title}}
        {{/post}}
    {{/get}}
    

Fetch all tags and output them using the [tags helper](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/tags)
.

    {{#get "tags" limit="100"}}{{tags}}{{/get}}
    

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#usage)

Usage
------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `{{#get}}` helper has several more options that greatly extend its functionality. The following section walks through these options and how to use them.

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#resources)

Resources
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The first parameter passed in is the name of the resource you want to query. Available resources include: `"posts"`, `"tags"`, `"authors"`, and `"tiers"`. **posts** - any published post **tags** - any tag that has a post associated with it **authors** - any author who has published a post **tiers** - any membership tier **newsletters** - any newsletter **Example:**

    {{#get "authors"}}
        {{! Loop through authors }}
        {{#foreach authors}}
            {{name}}
        {{/foreach}}
    {{/get}}
    

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#block-parameters)

Block parameters
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

As with the `{{#foreach}}` helper, use block parameters to rename your returned data collection to make it easier to reference or more distinguishable.

Block parameters are entered between pipe symbols (`|`)

The `{{#get}}` helper supports two parameters. The first entry refers to your returned data collection. The second entry refers to your [pagination object](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/pagination)
. **Block parameters example:** Get posts and rename the collection `articles`. The additional pagination object, `pages`, outputs the total number of posts in the collection.

    {{#get "posts" as |articles pages|}}
        {{! Loop through our articles collection }}
        {{#foreach articles}}
            {{title}}
        {{/foreach}}
        {{! Use the pages (pagination) object }}
        {{pages.total}}
    {{/get}}
    

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#using-else)

Using `{{else}}`
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All block helpers support the `{{else}}` helper, which outputs content when the first block doesn’t match. In the case of the `{{get}}` helper, this only happens if there’s an error and is mostly useful for debugging while developing. To output different content when there are no results returned from the `{{#get}}` request, use `{{else}}` with the `{{#foreach}}` helper.

    {{#get "posts" filter="featured:true"}}
        {{! Loop through our featured posts }}
        {{#foreach posts}}
            {{title}}
        {{else}}
        {{! If there are no featured posts}}
           <p>No posts!</p>
        {{/foreach}}
    {{else}}
      <p class="error">{{error}}</p>
    {{/get}}
    

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#attributes)

Attributes
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use `{{#get}}` helper attributes to specify which data is returned. Available attributes are identical to those used with the [Ghost Content API](https://docs.ghost.org/content-api#parameters)
. “Browse” requests (fetching multiple items) accept any or all of these attributes. “Read” requests (fetching a single item by **id** or **slug**) only accept the **include** attribute.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#limit)

_limit_

How many items to return Allowed values: 1-100 Default value: 15 Requesting more than 100 items will return a maximum of 100 items It’s possible to use the global `posts_per_page` setting, which is **5** by default. Configure the setting in the active theme’s `package.json` file. This global value is available via the `@config` global as `@config.posts_per_page`. **Examples:**

    {{! Get the 20 most recently published posts }}
    {{#get "posts" limit="20"}}{{/get}}
    
    {{! Use the posts_per_page setting}}
    {{#get "posts" limit=@config.posts_per_page}}{{/get}}
    

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#page)

_page_

when the total number of posts exceeds the number of post initially requested, the resulting collection from the `{{#get}}` query will be paginated. Choose which page of that collection you want to get with the `page` attribute. **Example:**

    {{! Get the 4th page of results.  In this case, where limit = 5, we are accessing posts 16 - 20}}
    {{#get "posts" limit="5" page="4"}}{{/get}}
    

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#order)

_order_

Specify how your data is ordered before being returned. You can choose any valid resource _field_ in ascending (`asc`) or descending (`desc`) order. **Examples:**

    {{! Get the 5 oldest posts }}
    {{#get "posts" limit="5" order="published_at asc"}}{{/get}}
    
    {{! Get posts in alphabetical order by title }}
    {{#get "posts" limit="5" order="title asc"}}{{/get}}
    

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#include)

_include_

By default, the `{{#get}}` helper will only fetch the base data from a resource. Use _include_ to expand the data that is returned. Separate multiple _include_ values with a comma. Base resource data:

*   **posts**
*   **tags**
*   **authors**
*   **tiers**

Include options for _Post_:

*   “authors” – adds author data
*   “tags – adds tag data

Include option for _Author_ and _Tag_

*   “count.posts” – adds the post count for each resource

Use `count.posts` to **order** your collection.

Include options for _Tiers_

*   “monthly\_price” - add monthly price data
*   “yearly\_price” – add yearly price data
*   “benefits” – add benefits data

**Examples:**

    {{! Get posts with author }}
    {{#get "posts" limit="5" include="authors"}}
        {{#foreach posts}}
            <span>Written by: {{authors}}</span>
        {{/foreach}}
    {{/get}}
    
    {{! Get posts with author and tags }}
    {{#get "posts" limit="5" include="authors,tags"}}
        {{#foreach posts}}
            <p>Written by: {{authors separator=", "}}</p>
            <p>keywords: {{tags separator=", "}}</p>
        {{/foreach}}
    {{/get}}
    
    {{! Get all tags and order them by post count }}
    {{#get "tags" limit="100" include="count.posts" order="count.posts desc"}}
        {{#foreach tags}}
            <p>{{name}} ({{count.posts}})</p>
        {{/foreach}}
    {{/get}}
    
    {{! Get all tiers with monthly price, yearly price, and benefits data }}
    {{#get "tiers" include="monthly_price,yearly_price,benefits" limit="100" as |tiers|}}
        {{! Loop through our tiers collection }}
        {{#foreach tiers}}
            {{name}}
            {{#if monthly_price}}
                <div>
                    <a href="javascript:" data-portal="signup/{{id}}/monthly">Monthly – {{price monthly_price currency=currency}}</a>
                </div>
            {{/if}}
            {{#if yearly_price}}
                <div>
                    <a href="javascript:" data-portal="signup/{{id}}/yearly">Yearly – {{price yearly_price currency=currency}}</a>
                </div>
            {{/if}}
            {{#if benefits}}
                {{#foreach benefits as |benefit|}}
                    {{benefit}}
                {{/foreach}}
            {{/if}}
        {{/foreach}}
    {{/get}}
    
    {{! Create a dynamic sign-up form that allows members to subscribe to specific newsletters}}
    <form data-members-form=>
      <input type="email" required data-members-email>
      {{#get "newsletters"}}
          {{#foreach newsletters}}
            <label>
              <input type="checkbox" value="{{name}}" data-members-newsletter />
    					{{name}}
            </label>
          {{else}}
      {{/get}}
      <button type="submit">Subscribe</button>
    </form>
    

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#filter)

_filter_

Use `filter` to make complex, logic-based queries on the data to fetch. In its most basic form, use `filter` to get posts that meet a simple boolean condition.

    {{! Only get posts that are featured }}
    {{#get "posts" limit="25" filter="featured:true"}}
        {{#foreach posts}}
            <a href="{{slug}}">{{title}}</a>
        {{/foreach}}
    {{/get}}
    

Specify multiple rules for the `filter` attribute by using `,` for _or_, `+` for _and_, and `-` for _negation_. It’s possible to check for booleans, match against strings, look for items within a group, and much more. For a full breakdown of the filtering syntax and how to use it, please see the [filter documentation in the API docs](https://docs.ghost.org/content-api#filtering)
.

#### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#passing-data-to-filter)

Passing data to `filter`

Data already available within your theme template can be passed to the `filter` attribute.

    {{! Get three more posts by the author of the current post when in post.hbs }}
    {{#post}}
        <h3><a href="{{url}}">{{title}}</a></h3>
        <section class="author-meta">
            <p>Post by: {{primary_author}}</p>
        </section>
        {{! Prevent the current post from being returned by filtering against its id }}
        {{#get "posts" filter="authors:{{primary_author.slug}}+id:-{{id}}" limit="3"}}
            <p>More posts by this author:
                <ol>
                    {{#foreach posts}}
                    <li><a href="{{url}}">{{title}}</a></li>
                    {{/foreach}}
                </ol>
            </p>
        {{/get}}
    {{/post}}
    

When passing `title`, `dates`, or other values with spaces to `filter`–wrap the data in single quotes.

    {{#post}}
        {{#get "posts" filter="published_at:<='{{published_at}}'+id:-{{id}}" limit="3"}}
        ...
        {{/get}}
    {{/post}}
    

Tip: To filter based on dates, use the data attributes, e.g.`{{published_at}}`, not the `{{date}}` helper, as helper functions do not get called inside of a filter.

#### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#filtering-by-primary-tag)

Filtering by primary tag

The `primary_tag` represents the first tag on a post. See the available [attributes](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/tags#list-of-attributes)
.

    {{! Get three posts that have the same primary tag as the current post}}
    {{#post}}
        {{#get "posts" filter="primary_tag:{{primary_tag.slug}}" limit="3"}}
            {{#foreach posts}}
                <li><a href="{{url}}">{{title}}</a></li>
            {{/foreach}}
        {{/get}}
    {{/post}}
    

#### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#filtering-by-primary-author)

Filtering by primary author

The `primary_author` represents the first author listed on a post. See the available [attributes](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/contexts/author#author-object-attributes)
.

    {{! Get three posts that have the same primary author as the current post}}
    {{#post}}
        {{#get "posts" filter="primary_author:{{primary_author.slug}}" limit="3"}}
            {{#foreach posts}}
                <li><a href="{{url}}">{{title}}</a></li>
            {{/foreach}}
        {{/get}}
    {{/post}}
    

#### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#filtering-by-membership-type)

Filtering by membership type

To restrict the type of tiers returned by the `{{#get}}` helper, filter the collection using the `type` attribute with either _free_ or _paid_.

    {{! Only get tiers that are paid}}
    {{#get "tiers" filter="type:paid"}}
        {{#foreach tiers}}
            <p>{{name}}</p>
        {{/foreach}}
    {{/get}}
    

#### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/get#filtering-by-tier-visibility)

Filtering by tier visibility

To restrict the visibility of tiers returned by the `{{#get}}` helper, filter the collection using the `visibility` attribute with either _public_ or _none_. Visibility here refers to whether the tier is selected or not in Portal settings.

    {{! Only get tiers that are public}}
    {{#get "tiers" filter="visibility:public"}}
        {{#foreach tiers}}
            <p>{{name}}</p>
        {{/foreach}}
    {{/get}}
    

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/functional/get.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/functional/get)

[foreach](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/foreach)
[has](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/functional/has)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Navigation

Utility

search

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Example Code](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/search#example-code)
    

* * *

The `{{search}}` helper outputs a search icon button that launches Ghost search when clicked. The color of the icon uses the `currentColor` CSS property, meaning it will match the color of text around it. The styling can be overriden by using the `.gh-search-icon` class plus `!important`.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/search#example-code)

Example Code

    {{search}}
    

The helper will output the following markup:

    <button class="gh-search-icon" aria-label="search" data-ghost-search style="display: inline-flex; justify-content: center; align-items: center; width: 32px; height: 32px; padding: 0; border: 0; color: inherit; background-color: transparent; cursor: pointer; outline: none;">
        <svg width="20" height="20" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M14.949 14.949a1 1 0 0 1 1.414 0l6.344 6.344a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 1.414l-6.344-6.344a1 1 0 0 1 0-1.414Z" fill="currentColor"/><path d="M10 3a7 7 0 1 0 0 14 7 7 0 0 0 0-14Zm-9 7a9 9 0 1 1 18 0 9 9 0 0 1-18 0Z" fill="currentColor"/></svg>
    </button>
    

For other ways to launch Ghost search and to learn more about this feature, [see the Ghost search documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/search)
.

# encode - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/encode#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Utility

encode

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

* * *

`{{encode}}` is a simple output helper which will encode a given string so that it can be used in a URL. The most obvious example of where this is useful is shown in Casper’s `post.hbs`, for outputting a twitter share link:

    <a class="icon-twitter" href="https://twitter.com/share?text={{encode title}}&url={{url absolute='true'}}"
        onclick="window.open(this.href, 'twitter-share', 'width=550,height=235');return false;">
        <span class="hidden">Twitter</span>
    </a>
    

Without using the `{{encode}}` helper on the post’s title, the spaces and other punctuation in the title will not be handled correctly.

# post_class - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/post_class#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Utility

post\_class

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Example Code](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/post_class#example-code)
    

* * *

`{{post_class}}` outputs classes intended for your post container, useful for targeting posts with styles. The classes are as follows:

*   `post` - All posts automatically get a `post` class.
*   `featured` - All posts marked as featured get the `featured` class.
*   `page` - Any static page gets the `page` class.
*   `tag-:slug` - For each tag associated with the post, the post get a tag in the format `tag-:slug`.

For example: A post which is not featured or a page, but has the tags `photo` and `panoramic` would get `post tag-photo tag-panoramic` as post classes. A featured post with a tag of `photo` would get `post tag-photo featured`. A featured page with a tag of `photo` and `panoramic` would get `post tag-photo tag-panoramic featured page`. Setting a post as featured or as a page can be done from the post settings menu.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/post_class#example-code)

Example Code

    <article class="{{post_class}}">
      {{content}}
    </article>
    

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/utility/post_class.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/utility/post_class)

[plural](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/plural)

# content - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/content#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Data

content

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Default CTA](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/content#default-cta)
    

* * *

`{{content}}` is a very simple helper used for outputting post content, when called within a `{{#post}}{{/post}}` [block expression](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/contexts/post#helpers)
. It makes sure that your HTML gets output correctly.

    <!-- post.hbs -->
    
    {{#post}}
    
    <article class="{{post_class}}">
      <section class="post-content">
        {{content}}
      </section>
    </article>
    
    {{/post}}
    

You can limit the amount of HTML content to output by passing one of the options: `{{content words="100"}}` will output just 100 words of HTML with correctly matched tags.

#### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/content#default-cta)

Default CTA

For visitors to members-enabled sites who don’t have access to the post in the current context, the `{{content}}` helper will output a [default upgrade/sign up CTA](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/members#default-cta)
.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/data/content.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/data/content)

[comments](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments)
[date](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/date)

# prev_post & next_post - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/prev_next_post#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Utility

prev\_post & next\_post

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

* * *

When in the scope of a post, you can call the next or previous post helper, which performs a query against the API to fetch the next or previous post in accordance with the chronological order of the site. Inside of the opening and closing tags of the `{{#next_post}}{{/next_post}}` or `{{#prev_post}}{{/prev-post}}` helper, the normal helpers for outputting posts will work, but will output the details of the post that was fetched from the API, rather than the original post.

    {{#post}}
    	{{#prev_post}}
    		<a href="{{url}}">{{title}}</a>
    	{{/prev_post}}
    
    	{{#next_post}}
    		<a href="{{url}}">{{title}}</a>
    	{{/next_post}}
    {{/post}}
    

You can also scope where to pull the previous and next posts from using the `in` parameter

    {{#post}}
    	{{#prev_post in="primary_tag"}}
    		<a href="{{url}}">{{title}}</a>
    	{{/prev_post}}
    
    	{{#next_post in="primary_tag"}}
    		<a href="{{url}}">{{title}}</a>
    	{{/next_post}}
    {{/post}}
    

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/utility/prev_next_post.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/utility/prev_next_post)

[post\_class](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/post_class)
[reading\_time](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/reading_time)

⌘I

# readable_url - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/readable_url#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Data

readable\_url

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

* * *

The `readable_url` helper outputs a human-readable URL by stripping out its protocol, www, query paramters, and hash fragments. It doesn’t strip out any subdomains or pathnames. This helper pairs well with the [`recommendations` helper](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/recommendations)
 to output more readable URLs. See the examples below to understand the helper’s expected output:

    {{readable_url "https://google.com"}}
    <!-- removes the "https://" protocol. Outputs: "google.com" -->
    
    {{readable_url "www.google.com"}}
    <!-- removes "www". Outputs: "google.com" -->
    
    {{readable_url "https://google.com?foo=bar&dog=love"}}
    <!-- removes query parameters. Outputs: "google.com" -->
    
    {{readable_url "https://google.com#section-1"}}
    <!-- removes hash fragments. Outputs: "google.com" -->
    
    {{readable_url "https://ghost.org/about"}}
    <!-- pathnames are not removed. Outputs: "ghost.org/about" -->
    
    {{readable_url "https://account.ghost.org"}}
    <!-- subdomains are not removed. Outputs: "account.ghost.org" -->
    

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/data/readable_url.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/data/readable_url)

[price](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/price)
[recommendations](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/recommendations)

⌘I

# log - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/log#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

Navigation

Utility

log

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

* * *

When running Ghost in development mode, you can use the `{{log}}` helper to output debug messages to the server console. In particular you can get handlebars to output the details of objects or the current context For example, to output the full ‘context’ that handlebars currently has access to: `{{log this}}` Or, to log each post in the loop:

    {{#foreach posts}}
       {{log post}}
    {{/foreach}}
    

If you’re developing a theme and running an install [using Ghost-CLI](https://docs.ghost.org/install/local)
, you must use `NODE_ENV=development ghost run` to make debug output visible in the console.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/utility/log.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/utility/log)

# partials - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/partials#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Utility

partials

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Example](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/partials#example)
    
*   [Partial properties](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/partials#partial-properties)
    
*   [Properties example](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/partials#properties-example)
    

* * *

`{{> "partials"}}` is a helper for reusing chunks of template code in handlebars files. This can be useful for any repeating elements, such as a post card design, or for splitting out components like a header for easier to manage template files. All partials are stored in the `partials/` directory of the theme. Partials will inherit context and make that context available within the partial file.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/partials#example)

Example

    {{#foreach posts}}
    
      {{> "post-card"}}
    
    {{/foreach}}
    

    <!-- partials/post-card.hbs -->
    <article class="post-card.hbs">
      <h2 class="post-card-title">
        <a href="{{url}}">{{title}}</a>
      </h2>
      <p>{{excerpt words="30"}}</p>
    </article>
    

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/partials#partial-properties)

Partial properties

Partials can take properties as well which provide the option to set contextual values per use case.

#### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/partials#properties-example)

Properties example

    {{> "call-to-action" heading="Sign up now"}}
    

    <!-- partials/call-to-action.hbs -->
    <aside>
      {{#if heading}}
        <h2>{{heading}}</h2>
      {{/if}}
      <form>
        <!-- ... -->
      </form>
    </aside>
    

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/utility/partials.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/utility/partials)

[pagination](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/pagination)

# @custom - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/custom#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Data

@custom

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Example code](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/custom#example-code)
    

* * *

The attributes of the `@custom` property are set by individual themes in the `package.json` file. Depending on the type of setting, the `@custom` property can then be used with the `{{#if}}` or `{{#match}}` helpers to customise the theme behaviour based on user settings.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/custom#example-code)

Example code

    <body class="{{body_class}} {{#match @custom.typography "Elegant serif"}}font-alt{{/match}}">
        ...
        <section class="footer-cta">
            {{#if @custom.cta_text}}<h2>{{@custom.cta_text}}</h2>{{/if}}
            <a href="#portal/signup">Sign up now</a>
        </section>
    </body>
    

More information about creating and working with custom theme settings can be found [here](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/custom-settings)
.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/data/custom.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/data/custom)

[@config](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/config)
[@page](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/page)

# excerpt - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/excerpt#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Data

excerpt

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

* * *

`{{excerpt}}` outputs content but strips all HTML. This is useful for creating excerpts of posts. If the post’s `custom_excerpt` property is set, then the helper will always output the `custom_excerpt` content ignoring the `words` & `characters` attributes. When both `html` and `custom_excerpt` properties are not set (for example, when member content gating strips the `html`) the output is generated from post’s `excerpt` property. You can limit the amount of text to output by passing one of the options: `{{excerpt characters="140"}}` will output 140 characters of text (rounding to the end of the current word).

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/data/excerpt.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/data/excerpt)

# split - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/split#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Utility

split

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Examples](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/split#examples)
    
*   [Block mode:](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/split#block-mode)
    
*   [Inline mode:](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/split#inline-mode)
    
*   [The separator attribute](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/split#the-separator-attribute)
    
*   [Additional examples](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/split#additional-examples)
    
*   [No empty strings](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/split#no-empty-strings)
    

* * *

The `{{#split}}` helper is designed to split a string into separate strings. It can be used in block or inline mode. The `{{#split}}` helper returns an array, suitable for iteration with `{{#foreach}}`, with individual elements of the array suitable for any helper that expects a string. Individual elements of the array may be addressed as `{{this}}` within a `{{#foreach}}` loop.

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/split#examples)

Examples
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/split#block-mode)

Block mode:

    {{#split "hello,world" as |elements|}}
      {{#foreach elements}}
        |{{this}}|
      {{/foreach}}
    {{/split}}
    
    Outputs:
    
    |hello||world|
    

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/split#inline-mode)

Inline mode:

    {{#foreach (split "hello, world" separator=",")}}
       {{this}} {{#unless @last}}<br>{{/unless}}
    {{/foreach}}
    
    Outputs:
    
    hello<br> world
    

`{{split}}` is designed for strings. If it receives a non-string, it attempts to convert it to a string first.

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/split#the-separator-attribute)

The separator attribute
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By default, strings are split at each ”,”. The `separator=""` attribute allows settings the split location to an arbitrary value. Passing an empty string for the separator results in splitting to single characters. Separators may be multiple characters.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/split#additional-examples)

Additional examples

    {{#foreach (split "my-slug-is-long-too-long" separator="-")}}
      {{#unless @first}}{{#unless @last}}-{{/unless}}{{/unless}}{{#unless @last}}
        {{this}}
      {{/unless}}
    {{/foreach}}
    
    Outputs: 
    
    my-slug-is-long-too
    
    

    {{#foreach (split "remove-this-from-my-slug" separator="remove-this-")}}
      {{this}}
    {{/foreach}}
    
    Outputs:
    
    from-my-slug
    

    {{!-- custom.list-of-tags is a comma-separated list like apple,banana,pear --}}
    {{#foreach (split @custom.list-of-tags)}} 
       {{> tag-loop slug=this}}
    {{/foreach}}
    

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/split#no-empty-strings)

No empty strings

Split filters the array to exclude any empty strings from the final result. Sequential separators will not result in empty strings.

    {{#foreach (split ",banana,,apple,")}}
      {{#unless @first}}{{#unless @last}}-{{/unless}}{{/unless}}{{#unless @last}}
        ({{this}})
      {{/unless}}
    {{/foreach}}
    
    Outputs: 
    
    (banana)(apple)
    
    Not: ()(banana)()(apple)() 
    

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/utility/split.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/utility/split)

[search](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/search)
[translate](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/translate)

# total_paid_members - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/total_paid_members#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Data

total\_paid\_members

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

* * *

The total\_paid\_members helper outputs a rounded number of total paid members from your Ghost publication in a human readable format. Example:

    {{total_paid_members}}
    

If you have 1225 paying members, it will output `1,200+`. For values above 100,000 it will output `100k+` and `3m+` respectively.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/data/total_paid_members.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/data/total_paid_members)

# @page - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/page#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Data

@page

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Example code](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/page#example-code)
    
*   [Styling tips when hiding the title and feature image](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/page#styling-tips-when-hiding-the-title-and-feature-image)
    

* * *

*   `@page.show_title_and_feature_image` - true (default) or false value from Ghost Editor

This toggle, only available for pages, lets users hide a page’s title and feature image to create pages that look radically different than posts (for example, full-width headers, CTAs, and landing pages). This setting is only available when using the [new Beta editor](https://ghost.org/changelog/editor-beta/)
. However, since the `@page.show_title_and_feature_image` is always present and defaults to `true`, supporting this feature in your theme won’t break anything for anyone using the old editor. Using the `@page` object is **not backward-compatible** with earlier versions of Ghost: once implemented the theme will only be compatible with Ghost 5.54.1 or later.

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/page#example-code)

Example code
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    {{#match @page.show_title_and_feature_image}}
    ...content...
    {{/match}}
    

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/page#styling-tips-when-hiding-the-title-and-feature-image)

Styling tips when hiding the title and feature image
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Whenever the page title and feature image are hidden, and the page content starts with a full-width card (such cards will have the class `.kg-width-full`), remove spacing between the top navigation and content (on pages only).
2.  Whenever multiple full-width cards are stacked, remove spacing between them (on posts and pages).
3.  Whenever content ends with a full-width card, remove spacing between the content and the footer (on pages only, posts often have additional content at the bottom such as comments, CTAs, related posts, etc.).

As a reminder, cards that have the ability to be set to full width are header cards, signup cards, image cards, and video cards. When an image or video has a caption, it will have the class `.kg-card-hascaption`, and maintaining spacing is desirable in this case. The implementation of these changes will look different on every theme. Find examples of these recommended changes in Casper [here](https://github.com/TryGhost/Casper/commit/d9c9390e17c1df1322ebfec774886058a56a0891)
 (1 and 3) and [here](https://github.com/TryGhost/Casper/blob/a60e3e976a341df462ba948d395bc52c37faffa4/assets/css/screen.css#L1345-L1348)
 (2).

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/data/page.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/data/page)

# comments - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Data

comments

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Basic example](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#basic-example)
    
*   [Attributes](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#attributes)
    
*   [Example with attributes](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#example-with-attributes)
    
*   [Comment count](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#comment-count)
    
*   [Attributes](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#attributes-2)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#examples)
    
*   [Additional customization](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#additional-customization)
    
*   [Advanced example](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#advanced-example)
    

* * *

The `{{comments}}`helper outputs Ghost’s member-based commenting system. [Learn more about comments.](https://ghost.org/help/commenting)
 Comments are visibleonly when they have been (1) enabled by the publication owner and (2) the person visiting the page has access to the post.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#basic-example)

Basic example

    {{comments}}
    

By default,`{{comments}}`outputs a title and comment count. These elements, along with the color mode and the saturation of the avatar’s background color, can be customized via attributes.

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#attributes)

Attributes
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Name | Description | Options | Default |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `title` | Header text for comment section | Any string | Member discussion |
| `count` | Boolean to toggle comment count on or off | `true` or `false` | `true` |
| `mode` | Set light or dark mode for comments | auto, light, or dark | auto (determined by the parent element’s CSS `color` property) |
| `saturation` | Set saturation of avatar background color | `number` | `60` |

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#example-with-attributes)

Example with attributes

    {{comments title="Join the club" count=false mode="light" saturation=80}}
    {{! Customizes header text, hides comment count, sets element to light mode and avatar background color saturation to 80% }}
    

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#comment-count)

Comment count
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use`{{comment_count}}`to output the number of comments a post has. This option is useful for displaying the comment count on the homepage or at the top of the post. Developers can also use it to customize the output of the`{{comments}}`helper.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#attributes-2)

Attributes

| Name | Description | Options | Default |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `singular` | The singular name for a comment | Any string | comment |
| `plural` | The plural name for comments | Any string | comments |
| `empty` | What to output when there are no comments | Any string | Output is empty when comment count equals zero |
| `autowrap` | Wraps comment count in an HTML tag | `HTML tag` or `false` | `span` |
| `class` | Add a custom class to wrapper element | Any string | ""  |

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#examples)

Examples

    {{comment_count empty="" singular="comment" plural="comments" autowrap="span" class=""}}
    {{! default output: <span>5 comments</span> }}
    
    {{comment_count singular="" plural=""}}
    {{! output: <span>5</span> }}
    
    {{comment_count empty="0"}}
    {{! output: <span>0</span>. (The default is an empty output.) }}
    
    {{comment_count autowrap="div" class="style-me"}}
    {{! output: <div class="style-me">5 comments</span> }}
    
    {{comment_count autowrap="false"}}
    {{! output: 5 comments (just text!) }}
    

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#additional-customization)

Additional customization
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use the `comments` helper with `{{#if}}` for more granular control over output. `{{#if comments}}` returns true when (1) comments have been enabled and (2) the reader has access to the post.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/comments#advanced-example)

Advanced example

    {{#if comments}}
       <h2>Discussion</h2>
       <a href="/guides">Community guidelines</a>
       {{comment_count}}
       {{comments title="" count=false mode="light" saturation=80}}
    {{/if}}
    

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/data/comments.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/data/comments)

[authors](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/authors)
[content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/content)

⌘I

# date - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/date#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

Navigation

Data

date

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Example Code](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/date#example-code)
    

* * *

`{{date}}` is a formatting helper for outputting dates in various formats. You can either pass it a date and a format string to be used to output the date like so:

    <!-- outputs something like 'July 11, 2016' -->
    {{date published_at format="MMMM DD, YYYY"}}
    

See the [Moment.js Display tokens](https://momentjs.com/docs/#/displaying/format/)
 for more options. Timezone and locale may be overridden from your site’s defaults by passing the `timezone` and `locale` parameters:

    <!-- outputs something like 'mar., 31 déc. 2013 22:58:58 +0100' -->
    {{date published_at locale="fr-fr" timezone="Europe/Paris"}}
    

Or you can pass it a date and the `timeago` flag:

    <!-- outputs something like '5 mins ago' -->
    {{date published_at timeago="true"}}
    

If you use the `timeago` flag on a site that uses caching - as on [Ghost(Pro)](https://ghost.org/pricing/)
 - dates will be displayed relative to when the page gets cached rather than relative to the visitor’s current time. If you call `{{date}}` without a format, it will default to a short localised format, `ll`. If you call `{{date}}` without telling it which date to display, it will default to one of two things:

1.  If there is a `published_at` property available (i.e. you’re inside a post object) it will use that
2.  Otherwise, it will default to the current date

`date` uses moment.js for formatting dates. See their documentation for a full explanation of all the different format strings that can be used.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/date#example-code)

Example Code

    <main role="main">
      {{#foreach posts}}
        <h2><a href="{{url}}">{{title}}</a></h2>
    
       <p>{{excerpt words="26"}}</p>
    
        {{!-- Here `published_at` is set, so this will show the article date --}}
        <time datetime="{{date format="YYYY-MM-DD"}}">{{date format="DD MMMM YYYY"}}</time>
      {{/foreach}}
    </main>
    <footer>
      {{!-- Here there is no `published_at` so this will show the current year --}}
      <p class="small">© {{date format="YYYY"}}</p>
    </footer>
    

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/data/date.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/data/date)

[content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/content)

# social_url - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/social_url#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Data

social\_url

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Examples](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/social_url#examples)
    

* * *

The `{{social_url}}` helper generates a URL for a specified social media platform based on the provided platform type. It takes a single argument, `type`, which specifies the social media platform (e.g., `facebook`, `mastodon`, etc.). The helper looks for the specified platform in the given context (usually author) and constructs the appropriate URL. For facebook and twitter, the helper will fall back to the sitewide values if they’re not set on the local context. For the remaining platforms the fallback behaviour is to output nothing. Supported platforms include: `facebook`, `twitter`, `linkedin`, `threads`, `bluesky`, `mastodon`, `tiktok`, `youtube`, `instagram`.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/social_url#examples)

Examples

Output the author’s Threads URL, using an `author` block:

    {{#author}}
      {{#if threads}}<a href="{{social_url type="threads"}}">Follow me on Threads</a>{{/if}}
    {{/author}}
    

Globally, Twitter and Facebook are available and can be accessed from anywhere in the theme.

    {{#if @site.twitter}}<a href="{{social_url type="twitter"}}">Follow us on Twitter</a>{{/if}}
    {{#if @site.facebook}}<a href="{{social_url type="facebook"}}">Follow us on Facebook</a>{{/if}}
    

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/data/social_url.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/data/social_url)

# reading_time - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/reading_time#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Utility

reading\_time

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Example Code](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/reading_time#example-code)
    
*   [Custom labelling](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/reading_time#custom-labelling)
    
*   [Example](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/reading_time#example)
    

* * *

`{{reading_time}}` renders the estimated reading time for a post. The helper counts the words in the post and calculates an average reading time of 275 words per minute. For the first image present, 12s is added, for the second 11s is added, for the third 10, and so on. From the tenth image onwards every image adds 3s. By _default_ the helper will render a text like this:

*   `x min read` for estimated reading time longer than one minute
*   `1 min read` for estimated reading time shorter than or equal to one minute

You can override the default text.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/reading_time#example-code)

Example Code

    {{#post}}
        {{reading_time}}
    {{/post}}
    

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/reading_time#custom-labelling)

Custom labelling
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Singular minute and plural minutes labelling can be customised using the options `minute` and `minutes`, using `%` as the plural minutes value.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/reading_time#example)

Example

    {{reading_time minute="Only a minute" minutes="Takes % minutes"}}
    

[See our full tutorial](https://ghost.org/tutorials/reading-time/)
 on how to customise and build upon the `reading_time` Handlebars helper.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/utility/reading_time.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/utility/reading_time)

[prev\_post & next\_post](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/prev_next_post)
[search](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/search)

# pagination - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/pagination#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Utility

pagination

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Pagination Attributes](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/pagination#pagination-attributes)
    
*   [Default Template](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/pagination#default-template)
    
*   [Unique helpers within this context](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/pagination#unique-helpers-within-this-context)
    

* * *

`{{pagination}}` is a template driven helper which outputs HTML for ’newer posts’ and ‘older posts’ links if they are available and also says which page you are on. You can override the HTML output by the pagination helper by placing a file called `pagination.hbs` inside of `content/themes/your-theme/partials`. Details of the default template are below. The data used to output the `{{pagination}}` helper is generated based on the post list that is being output (index, tag posts, author posts etc) and always exists at the top level of the data structure.

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/pagination#pagination-attributes)

Pagination Attributes
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **page** - the current page number
*   **prev** - the previous page number
*   **next** - the next page number
*   **pages** - the number of pages available
*   **total** - the number of posts available
*   **limit** - the number of posts per page

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/pagination#default-template)

Default Template
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The [default template](https://github.com/TryGhost/Ghost/blob/3d989eba2371235d41468f7699a08e46fc2b1e87/ghost/core/core/frontend/helpers/tpl/pagination.hbs)
 output by Ghost is shown below. You can override this by placing a file called `pagination.hbs` in the partials directory of your theme.

    <nav class="pagination" role="navigation">
        {{#if prev}}
            <a class="newer-posts" href="{{page_url prev}}">← Newer Posts</a>
        {{/if}}
        <span class="page-number">Page {{page}} of {{pages}}</span>
        {{#if next}}
            <a class="older-posts" href="{{page_url next}}">Older Posts →</a>
        {{/if}}
    </nav>
    

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/pagination#unique-helpers-within-this-context)

Unique helpers within this context
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `{{page_url}}` - accepts `prev`, `next` and `$number` to link to a particular page
*   `{{page}}` - outputs the current page number
*   `{{pages}}` - outputs the total number of pages

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/utility/pagination.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/utility/pagination)

[log](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/log)
[partials](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/partials)

⌘I

# plural - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/plural#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Utility

plural

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Examples](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/plural#examples)
    

* * *

`{{plural}}` is a formatting helper for outputting strings which change depending on whether a number is singular or plural. The most common use case for the plural helper is outputting information about how many posts there are in total in a collection. For example, themes have access to `pagination.total` on the homepage, a tag page or an author page. You can override the default text.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/plural#examples)

Examples

    {{plural pagination.total empty='No posts' singular='% post' plural='% posts'}}
    

`%` is parsed by Ghost and will be replaced by the number of posts. This is a specific behaviour for the helper.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/utility/plural.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/utility/plural)

[partials](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/partials)
[post\_class](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/post_class)

# meta data - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/meta_data#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Data

meta data

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

* * *

Ghost generates automatic meta data by default, but it can be overridden with custom content in the post settings menu. Meta data is output by default in [ghost\_head](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/ghost_head_foot)
, and can also be used in themes with the following helpers:

*   `{{meta_title}}` – the meta title specified for the post or page in the post settings
*   `{{meta_description}}` – the meta description specified for the post or page in the post settings
*   `{{canonical_url}}` – the custom canonical URL set for the post

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/data/meta_data.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/data/meta_data)

[link](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/link)
[navigation](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/navigation)

# total_members - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/total_members#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Navigation

Data

total\_members

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

* * *

The total\_members helper outputs a rounded number of total members from your Ghost publication in a human readable format. Example:

    {{total_members}}
    

If you have 1225 members, it will output `1,200+`. For values above 100,000 it will output `100k+` and `3m+` respectively.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/data/total_members.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/data/total_members)

[title](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/title)

# link - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/link#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Data

link

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Simple example](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/link#simple-example)
    
*   [Variables](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/link#variables)
    
*   [Simple variables example](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/link#simple-variables-example)
    
*   [Advanced variables example](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/link#advanced-variables-example)
    
*   [Dynamic attributes](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/link#dynamic-attributes)
    
*   [activeClass](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/link#activeclass)
    
*   [activeClass Example](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/link#activeclass-example)
    

* * *

`{{#link}}` is a block helper that creates links with dynamic classes. In its basic form it will create an anchor element that wraps around any kind of string, HTML or handlebars constructed HTML. With additional options it can have an active `class` or `target` behaviour, or `onclick` JavaScript events. A `href` attribute must be included or an error will be thrown.

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/link#simple-example)

Simple example
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    {{#link href="/about/"}}..linked content here..{{/link}}
    
    Will output:
    
    <a href="/about/">..linked content here..</a>
    

All attributes associated with the `<a></a>` element can be used in `{{#link}}`. Check out the MDN documentation on [the anchor element for more information](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/a)
.

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/link#variables)

Variables
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

Handlebars variables can be used for attribute values as well as strings. Variables do not need be wrapped with quotations:

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/link#simple-variables-example)

Simple variables example

    {{#link href=@site.url}}Home{{/link}}
    

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/link#advanced-variables-example)

Advanced variables example

    {{#foreach posts}}
      {{#link href=(url) class="post-link" activeClass="active"}}
        {{title}}
      {{/link}}
    {{/foreach}}
    

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/link#dynamic-attributes)

Dynamic attributes
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/link#activeclass)

`activeClass`

By default the active class outputted by `{{#link}}` will be `nav-current`, this is consistent with our [navigation helper](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/navigation)
. However it can be overwritten with the `activeClass` attribute:

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/link#activeclass-example)

`activeClass` Example

    {{#link href="/about/" activeClass="current"}}About{{/link}}
    
    When on the "/about/" URL it will output:
    
    <a href="/about/" class="current">About</a>
    

`activeClass` can also be given `false` value (`activeClass=false`), which will output an empty string. Effectively turning off the behaviour.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/data/link.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/data/link)

[img\_url](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/img_url)
[meta data](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/meta_data)

⌘I

# post - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/post#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Data

post

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Post Attributes](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/post#post-attributes)
    
*   [Static pages](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/post#static-pages)
    
*   [Featured posts](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/post#featured-posts)
    

* * *

When on a single post template such as `post.hbs` or `page.hbs`, outputting the details of your posts can be done with a block expression. The block expression `{{#post}}{{/post}}` isn’t strictly a ‘helper’. You can do this with any object in a template to access the nested attributes e.g. you can also use `{{#primary_author}}{{/primary_author}}` inside of the post block to get to the primary author’s name and other attributes. When inside a post list such as `index.hbs` or `tag.hbs` where there is more than one post, it is common to use the `{{#foreach post}}{{/foreach}}` to iterate through the list. When inside a `{{#foreach posts}}{{/foreach}}` or `{{#post}}{{/post}}` block (i.e. when inside the post scope), theme authors have access to all of the properties and helpers detailed on this page.

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/post#post-attributes)

Post Attributes
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The full list of post attributes and more information about outputting posts can be found in the post context documentation.

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/post#static-pages)

Static pages
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When outputting a static page, you can use the same `{{#post}}{{/post}}` block expression, and all the same helpers you can use for a post.

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/post#featured-posts)

Featured posts
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Featured posts get an extra class so that they can be styled differently. They are not moved to the top of the post list or displayed separately to the normal post list. Use `{{#if featured}}{{/if}}` to test if the current post is featured.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/data/post.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/data/post)

[navigation](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/navigation)
[price](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/price)

⌘I

# link_class - Ghost Developer Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/link_class#content-area)

[Ghost Developer Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=21b0a8eb2cb31ff62e99362023cc2de7)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/ghost/aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=aGR3I5_lq1oxakuc&q=85&s=bf70847c5fb515f7414edad80653b09d)](https://ghost.org/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Utility

link\_class

[Home](https://docs.ghost.org/)
[Documentation](https://docs.ghost.org/introduction)
[Migration Guides](https://docs.ghost.org/migration)

On this page

*   [Simple example](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/link_class#simple-example)
    
*   [activeClass](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/link_class#activeclass)
    
*   [class](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/link_class#class)
    
*   [Parent URLs](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/link_class#parent-urls)
    
*   [Example](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/link_class#example)
    

* * *

The `{{link_class}}` helper adds dynamic classes depending on the currently viewed page. If the page slug (e.g. `/about/`) matches the value given to the `for` attribute the helper will output a `nav-current` class. A `for` value must be provided.

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/link_class#simple-example)

Simple example
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    <li class="nav {{link_class for="/about/"}}">About</li>
    
    When on the "/about/" URL it will output:
    
    <li class="nav nav-current">About</li>
    
    By default it will output:
    
    <li class="nav ">About</li>
    

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/link_class#activeclass)

`activeClass`

By default the active class outputted by `{{link_class}}` will be `nav-current`, this is consistent with our [navigation helper](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/data/navigation)
. However it can be overwritten with the `activeClass` attribute:

    <li class="nav {{link_class for="/about/" activeClass="active"}}">About</li>
    
    Will output:
    
    <li class="nav active">About</li>
    

`activeClass` can also be given `false` value (`activeClass=false`), which will output an empty string. Effectively turning off the behaviour.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/link_class#class)

`class`

Optionally `{{link_class}}` can have additional active classes. Using the `class` attribute will add whatever value has been provided when the link is the active URL, `nav-current` (the default active class value) will be added last:

    <li class="nav {{link_class for="/about/" class="current-about"}}">About</li>
    
    Will output:
    
    <li class="nav current-about nav-current">About</li>
    

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/link_class#parent-urls)

Parent URLs
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Not only can `{{link_class}}` add active classes to current URLs, but it can also apply classes to parent URLs. If a user navigates to `/tags/toast/` then `{{link_class}}` can provide an active class to `/tags/` as well as `/tags/toast/`.

### 

[​](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/link_class#example)

Example

    <li class="nav {{link_class for="/tags/"}}">Tags</li>
    
    When on the "/tags/" URL it will output:
    
    <li class="nav nav-current">Tags</li>
    
    When on the "/tags/toast/" URL it will output:
    
    <li class="nav nav-parent">Tags</li>
    

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/edit/main/themes/helpers/utility/link_class.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/tryghost/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/themes/helpers/utility/link_class)

[ghost\_head & ghost\_foot](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/ghost_head_foot)
[log](https://docs.ghost.org/themes/helpers/utility/log)

⌘I
